# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =

type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #

  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)

# -1 if none is playing #

  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs

# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

    songs

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | Pause

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      |

  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id)

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)

  + AddSong(Id)

# -1 if none is playing #

  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      |

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | AddSong

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | AddSong(id)

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | AddSong(id) =>
        let songs, current

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | AddSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (play

    current

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | AddSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | AddSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)

        (playlist)

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Get all the song ids in the playlist #
let get_songs: PlayList -> [Id] =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    songs 
in

# Get the id of the currently playing song #
let get_current_song: PlayList -> Id =
  fun playlist ->
    let songs, current = playlist in
    current
in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun playlist, action ->
    case action
      | PlaySong(id) =>
        let songs, _ = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | PauseCurrentSong =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | RemoveSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
      | AddSong(id) =>
        let songs, current = playlist in
        (playlist)
    end
in
